### SSD constraints
SSD IFF (CR1_8xlarge OR HI1_4xlarge);
(NOT SSD) IFF (M2_xlarge OR CG1_4xlarge OR M1_large OR M1_xlarge OR M2_2xlarge OR M1_medium OR CC2_8xlarge OR M2_4xlarge OR M1_small OR C1_medium OR C1_xlarge);
